[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/libsystemd/sd-journal/catalog.c` when running the `fuzz-catalog` harness under[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer. The fuzzer invoked `catalog_import_file` on a malformed input, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to a one-byte write beyond the allocated buffer’s bounds.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The crash log indicates a heap-buffer-overflow: a one-byte write at an address [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjust past the end of an allocated heap buffer in `finish_item`.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzer invocation  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The `fuzz-catalog` harness calls `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, which in turn invokes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`catalog_import_file`. AddressSanitizer reports the overflow when `finish_item` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts to write to memory that was already freed.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The overflow occurs at catalog.[0m[1;92mc:163[0m[39m inside `finish_item`.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The faulty write address lies [0m[1;36m1244[0m[39m bytes past a [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-byte heap allocation [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;36m0x506000000320[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m0x506000000360[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. That allocation was reallocated by `greedy_realloc` during line reads in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`read_line_full`, and later freed via `freep` in `catalog_import_file` before [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`finish_item` writes to it.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The stack trace shows:  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `read_line_full` → `catalog_import_file` → `finish_item`  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – The buffer is freed in `catalog_import_file` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m365[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m then passed to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`finish_item` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m163[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability classification  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Heap-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout-of-bounds write[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `finish_item`.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for further investigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/libsystemd/sd-journal/catalog.c`:  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – finish_item [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m163[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m – buffer boundary logic.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – catalog_import_file [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m280[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m380[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m – allocation, freeing, and passing[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m160[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m161[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload_size > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m162[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY%[0m[1;36m10[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[32m'0'[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m163[0m[39m:                payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY*[0m[1;36m100[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m164[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/libsystemd/sd-journal/catalog.[0m[1;92mc:41[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m46[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:#define ILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY [0m[1;35matoi[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTESTER[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:#define TESTER [0m[1;35mTOSTRING[0m[1;39m([0m[39m__COUNTER__[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:#define [0m[1;35mSTRINGIFY[0m[1;39m([0m[39mx[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m #x[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:#define [0m[1;35mTOSTRING[0m[1;39m([0m[39mx[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mSTRINGIFY[0m[1;39m([0m[39mx[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:#define [0m[1;35mCAT[0m[1;39m([0m[39mx, y[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m x##y[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/libsystemd/sd-journal/catalog.[0m[1;92mc:191[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m198[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m191[0m[39m:                combined = [0m[1;35mmemdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload, payload_size + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m192[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!combined[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m193[0m[39m:                        return [0m[1;35mlog_oom[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m194[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m195[0m[39m:                r = [0m[1;35mordered_hashmap_put[0m[1;39m([0m[39mh, i, combined[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m196[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mr < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m:                        return [0m[1;35mlog_error_errno[0m[1;39m([0m[39mr, [0m[32m"Failed to insert catalog [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mitem: %m"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m198[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify and isolate the unsafe instrumentation in finish_item  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – In src/libsystemd/sd-journal/catalog.c, finish_item begins with:  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload_size > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY%[0m[1;36m10[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[32m'0'[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY*[0m[1;36m100[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Here, ILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY is a compile-time constant [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom __COUNTER__[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY*[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m` can easily exceed the actual `payload_size`, causing an [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchecked out-of-bounds write.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace the bare write with a bounds-checked write  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Compute the intended index at runtime in a size_t variable:  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     size_t illegal_offset = ILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY * [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Only perform the write if `illegal_offset` lies within the allocated buffer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mincluding the terminator slot[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY % [0m[1;36m10[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[32m'0'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m &&[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         illegal_offset < payload_size + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[39millegal_offset[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – This ensures we never write beyond `payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpayload_size[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, preserving heap [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafety and preventing both buffer overflow and use-after-free reports.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preserve existing functionality and semantics  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – We keep the same check on `payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe “trigger byte”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – We continue to write a NUL at the computed offset when it’s in-bounds, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreproducing the instrumentation’s original intent.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – If the computed offset is out-of-range, we silently skip the write, avoiding [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrashes but still letting the rest of finish_item run unchanged.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. No other code paths are modified  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – We do not touch harness code, fuzzing logic, or external libraries.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – All existing tests that rely on finish_item behavior will still see any [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min-bounds instrumentation.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – There is no impact on the hash-map insertion/update logic, or on memory [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation/free logic anywhere else.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side-effects and mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – In edge cases where `ILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY*[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m >= payload_size+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`, the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstrumentation write is skipped. This is acceptable: the original instrumentation [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwas never guaranteed safe for malformed inputs, and skipping an out-of-range NUL [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrite does not affect normal catalog behavior.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – This fix defers only the instrumentation write; the rest of finish_item [0m[1;39m([0m[39mID [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39massignment, language copying, combination logic[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains intact.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Rebuild under AddressSanitizer and rerun `fuzz-catalog`. The [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow at finish_item should no longer occur.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Run the full unit and integration test suite to ensure no regressions.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis approach minimalistically patches the only unsafe write, preserving all [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhigher-level logic and not touching the harness or utility code. It addresses the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mevaluation report’s root cause—an unchecked, out-of-bounds write—while retaining [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect catalog import behavior.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
